                  <foreign lang="ar">صَرْف</foreign> being thus used as an inf. n.; for the Arabs sometimes make the inf. n. fem., saying <foreign lang="ar">أَوْجَعَتْنِى ضَرْبُكَ</foreign> as well as <foreign lang="ar">أَوْجَعَنِى</foreign>
